                         <li data-reactid="684"><p data-reactid="685">I stayed here for 2 nights and would not recommend staying here unless you are very easy to please or else okay with packing and bringing your own bedding, maybe a chair or two and some hangers. The host is not much into cleanliness and shorts you on proper amenities. The one real plus is that the host provides an empty closet and a very comfortable mattress (Serta iComfort memory foam) which is very familiar to me since I own the king size version. However, they did not provide a complete bedding set for the bed and only 2 wire hangers. The host is nice and obviously desires their privacy and leaves the guest alone to enjoy theirs as well. The room provided is the on the first floor and very roomy but there was only one fold up chair provided to sit alone at a roomy dining table. There were constant strong East Indian food odors which was fine for me but might be a problem for some folks and I also ran into an individual staying in another room on the second floor of the home who seemed confused about the situation and had not actually met the host even after 3 weeks of staying there so you should be aware that others board there that do not use airbnb. </p><span data-reactid="686">Marie</span><span data-reactid="687">2017-03-09T00:00:00Z</span></li>

                        <div data-reactid="1105">
                         We call this room "The Egyptian" because of the distinctive textile on the wall. This is one of two rooms we rent at Adobe Horse Ranch in the Mountains. THE EGYPTIAN ROOM IS FOR FEMALE GUESTS ONLY! PLEASE READ THE DESCRIPTION CAREFULLY to make sure this room is a good fit for you!
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="1106">
                         I have two quiet and courteous female roommates who share the bathroom- because of this, I have to limit guests in this room to FEMALES ONLY! For a room that accommodates both genders, singles, couples, etc. please see my other listing "The Victorian at Adobe Horse Ranch" (private bath) . "The Egyptian" has a cozy queen bed with memory foam mattress, and a heated mattress pad for the winter. Plenty of closet space and desk/drawer storage. The room overlooks the garden courtyard and fountain. Walk to the quaint, one street western town along the famous Pacific Crest Trail which runs directly in front of our adobe castle on the hill. Quiet, high desert chaparral only minutes from major LA attractions. The best of both worlds! Please feel free to inquire even on blocked out days, as sometimes our schedule will open up unexpectedly! Our idyllic mountain hideaway is perfect for single and multiple night lodging, and ideal for visiting nurses working in the Antelope Valley, Santa Clarita or San Fernando Valleys. (Hospitals include Palmdale, Lancaster, Henry Mayo, and Olive View). The ranch is also a great stopover on your way to or from Las Vegas. 40 mi from Los Angeles/Burbank metro area, Universal Studios, 15 minutes from Magic Mountain theme park, and a little over an hour to Disneyland is a beautiful horse ranch nestled in a mountain valley, (a safe and quiet place to stay) the small town of Agua Dulce. The one- street town hosts the best Mexican restaurant in So Cal, a coffee shop and two bars with weekend bands. The Pacific Crest trail runs directly in front of the house, 1 mile to Vasquez Rocks park. The house is built around a garden courtyard with a fountain. There is a home gym with treadmill, weights, mirrors and television. We run a small horse rescue, White Fox Horse Rescue, and this is home for abused and abandoned horses. Free internet, plenty of parking. We have an assortment of continental breakfast items, tea and coffee. The White Fox Horse Rescue holds horse training and care classes for the community.. If you are a guest on the day we have a meetup, you are welcome to participate! For Vasquez Rocks hiking information, the internet has many resources. We also offer the following for additional fee- Personal trainer session in the gym, Horse Handling/Training sessions. Our English Shepherds, Elvis Presley and Paris Hilton, are here to welcome you!
                        </div>

                         quiet, mountainous high desert chaparral with estate sized ranches. Loads of white vinyl fence everywhere you look, although ours is brown because we are the rebels!
